93→    if match is None:\n    94→        # No frontmatter found at all -- leave file unchanged\n    95→        return 0\n    96→\n    97→    preamble = content[: match.start()]\n    98→    cleaned = 117→    The LLM cannot reliably produce execution timing or environment metadata,\n   118→    so the executor injects these fields post-subprocess (FR-033).\n   119→    \"\"\"\n   120→    content = output_file.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n   121→    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n   122→        return\n   123→\n   124→    # Find end of frontmatter\n   125→    end_idx =     )\n   168→\n   169→    # Inline embedding: read input files into the prompt instead of --file flags\n   170→    embedded = _embed_inputs(step.inputs)\n   171→    if embedded and )\n        effective_prompt = step.prompt\n        extra_args = [\n            arg\n            for input_path in step.inputs\n            for arg in (\"--file\", str(input_path))\n        ]\n The executor handles step ordering, retry logic,\n     5→parallel dispatch, and state management.\n     6→\n     7→NFR-007: No imports from superclaude.cli.sprint or superclaude.cli.roadmap.\n     8→\"\"\"\n     9→\n    10→from __future__ import annotations\n    11→\n    12→import logging\n    13→import threading\n    14→from datetime import datetime, timezone\n    15→from typing import Callable, Protocol\n    16→\n    17→from .gates import gate_passed\n    18→from .models import GateMode, PipelineConfig, Step, StepResult, StepStatus\n    19→from .trailing_gate import TrailingGateRunner\n    20→\n    21→_log = logging.getLogger(\"superclaude.pipeline.executor\")\n    22→\n    23→\n    24→class StepRunner(Protocol):\n    25→    \"\"\"Callable that executes a single step's subprocess and returns a result.\n    26→\n    27→    The runner is responsible for:\n    28→    - Launching the claude -p subprocess\n    29→    - Waiting for completion (with timeout enforcement)\n    30→    - Returning a StepResult with appropriate status\n    31→\n    32→    The runner is NOT responsible for:\n    33→    - Retry logic (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    34→    - Gate checking (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    35→    - Step ordering (handled by execute_pipeline)\n    36→    \"\"\"\n    37→\n    38→    def __call__(\n    39→        self,\n    40→        step: Step,\n    41→        config: PipelineConfig,\n    42→        cancel_check: Callable[[], bool],\n    43→    ) -> StepResult: ...\n    44→\n    45→\n    46→def execute_pipeline(\n    47→    steps: list[Step | list[Step]],\n    48→    config: PipelineConfig,\n    49→    run_step: StepRunner,\n    50→    on_step_start: Callable[[Step], None] = lambda s: None,\n    51→    on_step_complete: Callable[[Step, StepResult], None] = lambda s, r: None,\n    52→    on_state_update: Callable[[dict], None] = lambda state: None,\n    53→    cancel_check: Callable[[], bool] = lambda: False,\n    54→    trailing_runner: TrailingGateRunner | None = None,\n    55→) -> list[StepResult]:\n    56→    \"\"\"Generic pipeline executor.\n    57→\n    58→    Processes steps in order. Each element in ``steps`` is either:\n    59→    - A single Step (executed sequentially)\n    60→    - A list[Step] (all steps in the list executed in parallel)\n    61→\n    62→    For each step:\n    63→    1. Call on_step_start(step)\n    64→    2. Call run_step(step, config, cancel_check)\n    65→    3. If step has gate criteria: run gate_passed()\n    66→       - BLOCKING mode: evaluate synchronously, halt on failure\n    67→       - TRAILING mode (grace_period > 0): submit to TrailingGateRunner,\n    68→         continue execution; sync point at end collects results\n    69→    4. If gate fails and attempts < retry_limit: retry (go to 2)\n    70→    5. If gate fails and attempts exhausted: HALT\n    71→    6. Call on_step_complete(step, result)\n    72→    7. Call on_state_update(updated_state_dict)\n    73→\n    74→    For parallel step groups:\n    75→    - All steps in the group run concurrently via _run_parallel_steps()\n    76→    - If any step in the group fails, remaining steps are cancelled\n    77→    - All results from the group must be PASS before proceeding\n    78→\n    79→    Returns list of all StepResults (one per step, flattened).\n    80→    \"\"\"\n    81→    all_results: list[StepResult] = []\n    82→    # Create trailing runner if grace_period > 0 and none provided\n    83→    _trailing = trailing_runner\n    84→    if _trailing is None and config.grace_period > 0:\n    85→        _trailing = TrailingGateRunner()\n    86→\n    87→    for entry in steps:\n    88→        if cancel_check():\n    89→            break\n    90→\n    91→        if isinstance(entry, list):\n    92→            # Each element in ``steps`` is either:\n    - A single Step (executed sequentially)\n    - A list[Step] (all steps in the list executed in parallel)\n\n    For each step:\n    1. If step has gate criteria: run gate_passed()\n       - BLOCKING mode: evaluate synchronously, halt on failure\n       - TRAILING mode (grace_period > 0): submit to TrailingGateRunner,\n         continue execution; sync point at end collects results\n    4. Returns when all complete or one fails.\n\n    Cross-cancellation: if any step fails after retry, a shared Event\n    is set, causing remaining steps to terminate their subprocesses.\n    \"\"\"\n    cancel_event = threading.Event()\n    results: list[StepResult | None] = [None] * len(steps)\n\n    def _worker(idx: int, step: Step) -> None:\n        def combined_cancel() -> bool:\n            return cancel_check() or cancel_event.is_set()\n\n        result = _execute_single_step(step, config, run_step, combined_cancel)\n        results[idx] = result\n        if result.status != StepStatus.PASS:\n            cancel_event.set()\n\n    threads = [\n        threading.Thread(target=_worker, args=(i, s), daemon=True)\n        for i, s in enumerate(steps)\n    ]\n    for t in threads:\n        t.start()\n    for t in threads:\n        t.join()\n\n    #    input_paths: list[Path],\n) -> list[Step | list[Step]]:\n    \"\"\"Build steps for multi-agent validation.\n\n    N agents -> N parallel reflections -> gate each -> adversarial merge.\n    \"\"\"\n \"info_count\": 0}\n\n    if not report_path.exists():\n        return result\n\n    content = report_path.read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")\n    if not content.startswith(\"---\"):\n        return result\n\n    end_idx = content.find(\"\\n---\", 3)\n    if end_idx == -1:\n        return result\n\n    frontmatter = content[3:end_idx]\n    for line in frontmatter.splitlines():\n        line = line.strip()\n        if \":\" not in line:\n            continue\n        key, _, val = line.partition(\":\")\n        key = key.strip()\n        val = val.strip()\n        if key == \"blocking_issues_count\":\n            try:\n                result[\"blocking_count\"] = int(val)\n            except ValueError:\n                pass\n        elif key == \"warnings_count\":\n            try:\n                result[\"warning_count\"] = int(val)\n            except ValueError:\n                pass\n\n    # Count INFO findings from body\n    body = content[end_idx + 4:]  # skip closing ---\n    info_count = 0\n    for line in body.splitlines():\n        if \"[INFO]\" in line:\n            info_count += 1\n    result[\"info_count\"] = info_count\n\n    return result\n\n\ndef by agent count\n    if len(config.agents) == 1:\n        steps = _build_single_agent_steps(config, validate_dir, input_paths)\n    else:\n        steps = _build_multi_agent_steps(config, validate_dir, failures = [r for r in results if r.status in (StepStatus.FAIL, StepStatus.TIMEOUT)]\n    if failures:\n        _log.error(\n            \"Validation pipeline halted: %d step(s) failed\",\n
